msg:This time I took my parents-in-law out, thinking of avoiding the crowds, and booked the Anlan Hotel, which is far away from the central scenic area of ‚Äã‚ÄãQiandao Lake.

Maybe because the hotel has only more than 80 rooms, the check-in process is very fast and there is no need to wait, and the hotel front desk has contacted us the day before to inform us that they will arrange a nearby room, indicating that they have arranged the room in advance. On the day of check-in, the room of my parents-in-law was upgraded for free.

After paying the deposit, the hotel battery car will take us to the room. Although it is a single-family villa, the room is not big, but the scenery is very good, and every window is like a painting.

Although the breakfast is not particularly varied, it is also rich, especially tasting the natural honey of Qiandao Lake, which is produced by the hotel's own bees. In addition, the hotel provides welcome fruits, mini bar, and different goodnight desserts every night.

The overall environment of the hotel is very quiet and comfortable, but the villa is relatively low, the view is not wide, and the archipelago cannot be seen. In addition, the spa island is also relatively far away, and it will be empty if you don't make an appoin**ent, but the scenery of the spa island is more surprising than the island where the hotel room is located.

The hotel staff are also very enthusiastic, and they will take the initiative to introduce the hotel and local customs when you ask questions. All in all, the overall stay experience was quite satisfactory.

msg:The first time I came to Qiandao Lake, I chose the Qiandao Lake Anlan Hotel, the best on Ctrip, and stayed for two nights. The experience was good.

1. Decoration style
The style throughout the day belongs to the Hui-style architecture, which echoes the Qiandao Lake scenic spot, and really has the feeling of a Jiangnan water town;

2. Cruise ship
The package includes a boat trip to Thousand Island Lake. Because there are few people, it is basically the same as a charter boat, and the experience is still very good;

3. Meals
Because there are few guests, breakfast is a la carte and of good quality. The dinner dishes are unique to Qiandao Lake, and the fish head soup is also delicious;

4. Service
The service staff is always available, well-trained and very polite.

5. Location
The only drawback is that the location is too remote, and traveling at the same time requires a car to pick up and drop off, which is a bit troublesome. Due to the small number of guests, Shuxiang Pavilion and other facilities are not open, and there are no gyms and other facilities.

In short, the overall quality is very good. I recommend this Qiandao Lake hotel to everyone.

Then there are a lot of disadvantages! ! In short, the team is playing badly.
1. There is no call center. If there is a need after late at night, it is basically a front desk or concierge (small resort hotels can understand).
2. The two-bedroom villa booked was not confirmed by phone in advance! It was confirmed twice when I arrived at the hotel very late! There was no butler to connect and serve during the whole stay, which I don‚Äôt understand! Not to mention arranging various activities, nothing!
3. When the car arrived at the door of the hotel, the concierge did not take the initiative to open the door and ask if the luggage needed to be moved every time. Several times, he stood there and watched motionless.
4. We traveled in off-peak hours. When there were no guests in CI and CO, the two receptionists at the front desk had no habit of getting up to greet the guests every time they saw them come in. They sat there all the time, not to mention welcome tea and towels. A total of two nights were booked. When cleaning the next day after staying for one night, the cleaning aunt was told by the front desk that we would check out today, which was really confusing. The front desk service and ability of Anlan are not as good as those of a guesthouse. The whole trip experience is greatly deducted.
5. Then there is the food and beverage. The free meal, except for the fish head, fried lettuce and fried rice, is freshly fried. Other dishes are either pre-made or pre-processed for a long time. If it is a meal of this quality, it is better not to send it. Do you think that the guests staying in Anlan have such a bad taste and are so easy to fool? In addition, if you order a la carte, the price is outrageous, with this product, thank you very much.

In the end, I heard that the hotel just changed its brand from Anlu to Anlan in early 24 years. The team and hardware have basically not changed. Maybe only the price has been adjusted. Qiandao Lake Anlan does not have any rivals in this price range of hotels, but if the management continues to maintain such a poor front office and Chinese restaurant team, then the regular customers of this Anlan will only decrease.

msg:A great family vacation experience.
During the Spring Festival in Hangzhou, there are crowds of people everywhere, and I really don‚Äôt want to join in the fun.
I have known about this hotel before. It used to be called Anlu. It is a luxury resort hotel. It is located on the west side of the central lake area away from Qiandao Lake. It is more convenient to drive by yourself.
The overall design of the hotel reflects the Hui-style architecture of the Jiangnan water town. It is located on a peninsula. The rooms are all independent courtyards with viewing terraces. Qiandao Lake is outside the window. Although this season is the dry season, the overall scenery is still very good. The hotel's privacy is very good, especially suitable for vacation and relaxation.
The entire park provides battery car services, which are available at any time and provide timely and thoughtful service.
The hotel's facilities are also very complete, including a Chinese restaurant, a food gallery, a book bar and a spa.
The outdoor swimming pool cannot be used in winter, so there is an indoor swimming pool.
The spa place is on another peninsula next to the hotel. It is about 2 kilometers away by electric car. The scenery along the way is very beautiful.
The breakfast is generally good, with a rich variety and some local snacks. The Chinese restaurant provides local delicacies from Qiandao Lake, with fresh ingredients, authentic taste, and long business hours.
It is also more convenient to park if you drive by yourself. It is about 45 kilometers from the Qiandao Lake exit of the expressway to the hotel, but because of the high speed limit on the road, it takes about an hour to drive. The hotel's main parking lot is about 400 meters away from the lobby, and the hotel also thoughtfully provides a battery car pick-up service. The parking lot is equipped with 5 new energy slow chargers, making it more convenient to drive an electric car.
It is adjacent to Wenyuan Lion City (an antique town). It is about 2 kilometers away by car, which is very convenient. There is also the Qinchuan Ancient Town, about 10 kilometers away from the hotel. It is a place where the local aborigines live, and it still has a quite local style.
The overall feeling is good. I will come back next time when the spring flowers are blooming.

There is a big problem with the food hygiene and environmental hygiene of this hotel. After breakfast, I suffered from vomiting and diarrhea. Two of the six people I traveled with suffered from vomiting and diarrhea. After struggling all morning, I took medicine on my own after vomiting and defecation, so I judged that there was a problem with food hygiene. The hotel's handling methods are very unprofessional and sincere to the guests. They are: drinking a glass of juice to prove to you that she is fine, so the juice is fine, verbally caring about whether she is not in good health and cannot eat cold food, and then giving cookies and room coupons. , and also mail specialties from Qiandao Lake. But I will never admit that it is a hotel problem. Only after I complained to 12315 did I find out that they were very professional in handling food safety in their hotel and were professional habitual offenders. Their judgment was definitely not so skilled and accurate just because it happened once or twice. Their purpose of doing this is to delay time, and they have already expected you to file a complaint with the government depar**ent (Chun'an looks like a food safety city from the billboards on the street), and they will destroy the food and other evidence involved as soon as possible. (Government staff told me that the correct thing for a hotel to do is to keep a sample as soon as possible after receiving a food safety complaint. The hotel obviously knew it, but went in another direction) After time, you will be better, vomit and feces There is no evidence waiting for you to identify it yourself. The government depar**ent did not have first-hand evidence, so they mediated, and the hotel provided room vouchers. I am still very angry and can only send them dirty words. The above are food hygiene issues. Next is environmental sanitation: I originally made a reservation for two days, but after checking in, I found that the dust on the upper board of the wardrobe was very thick (the upper board of the wardrobe was high, so the waiter probably couldn‚Äôt reach too far inside). At that time, I wondered if there was no one living in this room. But forget it. The next morning at about 6 o'clock, I was woken up by the smell. I thought it was the smell of sewers. I woke up and said I would go for a run by the lake. When I opened the door, the outdoor doorway smelled much worse than the inside. I figured it was a septic tank leak or something. So I immediately (around 6:30) applied to Ctrip to check out one day early. So he has to pay in advance and the settings like not being able to cancel are all pitfalls.
